<script>
	function getFBCustomerData() {
				var customerData = {};
				if (mpro.Visitor) {
			customerData.external_id = mpro.Visitor.getId();
		}
		return customerData;
	}

	function getFBCookieData() {
		var cookieData = document.cookie.split(';');
		
		var fbp = cookieData
			.map(c => c.trim())
			.filter(c => c.startsWith('_fbp='))
			.map(c => c.split('_fbp=')[1].trim())[0] ?? null;
		
		var rawFbc = cookieData
			.map(c => c.trim())
			.filter(c => c.startsWith('_fbc='))
			.map(c => c.split('_fbc=')[1].trim())[0] ?? null;
		var fbc = null;

		// Validate fbc timestamp — discard if stale (> 90 days) or malformed
		if (rawFbc) {
			var parts = rawFbc.split('.');
			if (parts.length >= 4) {
				var clickTs = parseInt(parts[2], 10);
				var ageMs = Date.now() - clickTs;
				var maxAge = 90 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
				if (!isNaN(clickTs) && ageMs >= 0 && ageMs <= maxAge) {
					fbc = rawFbc;
				}
			}
		}

		// Fall back to fbclid in the URL if no valid cookie fbc
		if (!fbc) {
			try {
			var fbclid = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('fbclid');
			if (fbclid && /^[A-Za-z0-9_-]+$/.test(fbclid)) {
				fbc = 'fb.1.' + Date.now() + '.' + fbclid;
			}
			} catch(e) {}
		}

		return { fbp: fbp, fbc: fbc };
	}

	function fbcapi(event, eventData, eventID, customerData) {

				mpro.push(function() {

						if (!customerData) {
				customerData = getFBCustomerData();
			}

						if (customerData && mpro.Visitor && (customerData.external_id == null)) {
				customerData.external_id = mpro.Visitor.getId();
			}

						var resolvedEventID = eventID ?? "MP" + Date.now();

						fbq('track', event, eventData, {'eventID': resolvedEventID});
			console.log('facebook_pixel', event, eventData, resolvedEventID, customerData);

								});
	}
</script>

				<script>(function(){
				const isSupported = CSS.supports('aspect-ratio', '1 / 1');
				if (!isSupported) {
					const ratioContainers = document.querySelectorAll('[data-ratio]');
					[...ratioContainers].forEach((container) => {
						container.style.paddingTop = ((100 / container.dataset.ratio) + '%');
						container.style.aspectRatio = 'unset';
						container.style.position = 'relative';

						// Fix product page thumbs
						if (container.classList.contains('product-summary__thumb-image-wrapper')) {
							const parent = container.parentElement;
							var computedStyle = getComputedStyle(parent);

							container.style.width = (parent.clientHeight - parseFloat(computedStyle.paddingTop) - parseFloat(computedStyle.paddingBottom)) * container.dataset.ratio + 'px';
						}

						const images = container.querySelectorAll('img');
						[...images].forEach((image) => {
							image.style.width = '100%';
							image.style.height = '100%';
							image.style.position = 'absolute';
							image.style.aspectRatio = 'unset';
							image.style.top = 0;
							image.style.left = 0;
							image.style.objectFit = 'contain';
						});
					});
				}
			})();</script>
